<script>
// ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
var D=null, viewMode='ytd', pyrMode='ytd', envMode='conso';
var tagStatFilter='all';
var clnStatFilter='all';
var charts={};
var ML=['Jan','Fév','Mar','Avr','Mai','Jun','Jul','Aoû','Sep','Oct','Nov','Déc'];
var C={p1:'#09637e',p2:'#0a7a9a',p3:'#0b91b5',p4:'#0da8d2',
  red:'#e8445a',amber:'#f5a623',green:'#10c985',
  purple:'#8b5cf6',teal:'#14b8a6',orange:'#f97316',
  grid:'rgba(26,64,85,0.65)',txt:'#4d8a9a'};
var BASE={responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,
  plugins:{legend:{display:false}},
  scales:{x:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:10}}},
          y:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:10}}}}};

// Dates
var TODAY_ISO='', TOMORROW_ISO='';
// Renvoie la date au format ISO « yyyy-MM-dd » en HEURE LOCALE.
// Indispensable : Date.toISOString() convertit en UTC, ce qui décale
// d'un jour les dates stockées à minuit local en GMT+1 (Algérie).
// Ex. : 28/05/2026 00:00 GMT+1 → '2026-05-27' via toISOString → BUG.
function localIso(d){
  if(!(d instanceof Date)||isNaN(d.getTime())) return '';
  var y=d.getFullYear();
  var m=String(d.getMonth()+1); if(m.length<2) m='0'+m;
  var dd=String(d.getDate());   if(dd.length<2) dd='0'+dd;
  return y+'-'+m+'-'+dd;
}
(function(){
  var n=new Date(); TODAY_ISO=localIso(n);
  var t=new Date(n); t.setDate(t.getDate()+1); TOMORROW_ISO=localIso(t);
})();
function diffDays(iso1,iso2){ return Math.round((new Date(iso1)-new Date(iso2))/(86400000)); }

// ══ THÈME ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════
var isLight=false;
function toggleTheme(){
  isLight=!isLight;
  document.documentElement.classList.toggle('light',isLight);
  document.getElementById('themeBtn').textContent=isLight?'☀️':'🌙';
  C.grid=isLight?'rgba(9,99,126,.1)':'rgba(26,64,85,0.65)';
  C.txt=isLight?'#2d5a72':'#4d8a9a';
  BASE.scales.x.grid.color=C.grid; BASE.scales.x.ticks.color=C.txt;
  BASE.scales.y.grid.color=C.grid; BASE.scales.y.ticks.color=C.txt;
  if(D){ updateC1();updateC2();updateEnvCharts();applyIncF();applyTagF();applyAccF();renderPyramid(); }
  try{ localStorage.setItem('hse_theme',isLight?'light':'dark'); }catch(e){}
}
(function(){ try{ if(localStorage.getItem('hse_theme')==='light'){isLight=false;toggleTheme();} }catch(e){} })();

// ══ NAVIGATION ════════════════════════════════════════════════
function goTab(id,el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(function(p){p.classList.remove('on');});
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t){t.classList.remove('on');});
  document.getElementById(id).classList.add('on'); el.classList.add('on');
}
function goAI(){
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t,i){t.classList.toggle('on',i===5);});
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(function(p){p.classList.remove('on');});
  document.getElementById('ai').classList.add('on');
}
function goVeille(){
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(function(t,i){t.classList.toggle('on',i===6);});
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(function(p){p.classList.remove('on');});
  document.getElementById('veille').classList.add('on');
}

// ══ MODALS ════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function openModal(id){ document.getElementById(id).style.display='flex'; document.body.style.overflow='hidden'; }
function closeModal(id){ document.getElementById(id).style.display='none'; document.body.style.overflow=''; }
document.addEventListener('keydown',function(e){
  if(e.key==='Escape') ['incModal','accModal','tagModal','cleanModal','clnPlanModal','clnProductsModal','clnEmbedModal'].forEach(function(id){closeModal(id);});
});
function switchTab(prefix,tab,el){
  var panel=el.closest('.modal-panel');
  panel.querySelectorAll('[id^="'+prefix+'-"]').forEach(function(d){d.style.display='none';});
  panel.querySelectorAll('.modal-tab').forEach(function(t){t.classList.remove('on');});
  document.getElementById(prefix+'-'+tab).style.display='block'; el.classList.add('on');
}

// ══ NOTIFICATIONS ════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildNotifications(){
  if(!D||!D.planning) return;
  var todayItems=[], tomorrowItems=[], fumigWarn=[];
  D.planning.forEach(function(p){
    if(!p.isoDate) return;
    var isFumig=p.fumigation||p.activite.toLowerCase().indexOf('fumig')>-1;
    if(p.isoDate===TODAY_ISO) todayItems.push(p);
    else if(p.isoDate===TOMORROW_ISO) tomorrowItems.push(p);
    if(isFumig&&p.isoDate>TODAY_ISO){
      var j=diffDays(p.isoDate,TODAY_ISO);
      if(j>=1&&j<=6) fumigWarn.push({p:p,jours:j});
    }
  });
  var totalNormal=todayItems.length+tomorrowItems.length;
  var badge=document.getElementById('notifBadge');
  if(totalNormal>0){badge.textContent=totalNormal>9?'9+':String(totalNormal);badge.classList.add('show');}
  else badge.classList.remove('show');
  var badgeFum=document.getElementById('notifBadgeFum');
  if(fumigWarn.length>0) badgeFum.classList.add('show'); else badgeFum.classList.remove('show');
  var total=totalNormal+fumigWarn.length;
  document.getElementById('notifCount').textContent=total+' événement'+(total>1?'s':'');
  var list=document.getElementById('notifList');
  if(total===0){
    list.innerHTML='<div class="notif-empty">✅ Aucun événement aujourd\'hui ni demain</div>';
  } else {
    var html='';
    fumigWarn.forEach(function(fw){
      html+='<div class="notif-item fumig-warn"><span class="notif-lbl lbl-fumig">🦟 FUMIGATION J-'+fw.jours+'</span>'
        +'<div class="notif-act">'+esc(fw.p.activite)+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-det">'+esc(fw.p.details)+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-date">📅 '+fw.p.date+'</div></div>';
    });
    todayItems.forEach(function(p){
      html+='<div class="notif-item today"><span class="notif-lbl lbl-today">📅 Aujourd\'hui</span>'
        +'<div class="notif-act">'+esc(p.activite)+(p.fumigation?' 🦟':'')+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-det">'+esc(p.details)+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-date">'+p.date+'</div></div>';
    });
    tomorrowItems.forEach(function(p){
      html+='<div class="notif-item tomorrow"><span class="notif-lbl lbl-tomorrow">📅 Demain</span>'
        +'<div class="notif-act">'+esc(p.activite)+(p.fumigation?' 🦟':'')+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-det">'+esc(p.details)+'</div>'
        +'<div class="notif-date">'+p.date+'</div></div>';
    });
    list.innerHTML=html;
  }
  // Alerte fumigation Vue Globale
  var alert=document.getElementById('fumigAlert');
  var fumigToday=todayItems.filter(function(p){return p.fumigation;});
  if(fumigToday.length>0){
    alert.classList.add('show');
    document.getElementById('fumigTitle').textContent='🦟 FUMIGATION AUJOURD\'HUI';
    document.getElementById('fumigSub').innerHTML='<strong>'+esc(fumigToday[0].activite)+'</strong> — Préparez toutes les zones.';
  } else if(fumigWarn.length>0){
    fumigWarn.sort(function(a,b){return a.jours-b.jours;});
    var fw=fumigWarn[0];
    alert.classList.add('show');
    document.getElementById('fumigTitle').textContent='🦟 Fumigation dans '+fw.jours+' jour'+(fw.jours>1?'s':'');
    document.getElementById('fumigSub').innerHTML='<strong>'+esc(fw.p.activite)+'</strong> prévue le <strong>'+fw.p.date+'</strong>.'
      +(fw.jours<=2?' <span style="color:var(--red);font-weight:700">— PRÉPARATION URGENTE</span>':'');
  } else alert.classList.remove('show');
}
function toggleNotif(){ document.getElementById('notifPanel').classList.toggle('open'); }
document.addEventListener('click',function(e){
  var wrap=document.getElementById('notifWrap');
  if(wrap&&!wrap.contains(e.target)) document.getElementById('notifPanel').classList.remove('open');
});

// ══ HELPERS ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
function mkChart(id,type,labels,datasets,opts){
  if(charts[id]) charts[id].destroy();
  try{ charts[id]=new Chart(document.getElementById(id),{type:type,data:{labels:labels,datasets:datasets},options:opts||BASE}); }catch(e){}
}
function kpiCard(lbl,val,color,sub,cls,pct,bc){
  var bar='';
  var dv=(typeof val==='number')?fmtNum(val):val;
  if(pct!=null){ bar='<div class="kpi-bar"><div class="kpi-bar-fill" style="width:'+Math.min(pct,100)+'%;background:'+bc+'"></div></div><div class="kpi-pct" style="color:'+bc+'">'+fmtNum(Math.min(pct,100))+'% obj.</div>'; }
  return'<div class="kpi '+cls+'"><div class="kpi-lbl">'+lbl+'</div><div class="kpi-val '+color+'">'+dv+'</div><div class="kpi-sub">'+sub+'</div>'+bar+'</div>';
}
function prog(lbl,val,tgt,lower,isPct){
  if(val===null||val===undefined) return'';
  if(!tgt||tgt===0) tgt=1;
  var pct=Math.min(Math.round(Math.abs(val)/Math.abs(tgt)*100),100);
  var ok=lower?val<=tgt:val>=tgt;
  var tc=ok?'ok':(pct>60?'warn':'bad'), bc=ok?'bg':(pct>60?'ba':'br');
  return'<div class="prow"><div class="phdr"><span class="plbl">'+lbl+'</span><span class="pnum '+tc+'">'+(isPct?fmtNum(val)+'%':fmtNum(val))+'</span></div><div class="pbg"><div class="pb '+bc+'" style="width:'+pct+'%"></div></div></div>';
}
function cleanMd(t){ if(!t||t==='null')return''; return t.replace(/\*\*/g,'').replace(/\*/g,'').replace(/#+\s*/g,'').replace(/\\n/g,'\n').replace(/\\-/g,'-').trim(); }
function cleanMonths(arr,hdrs){
  var lbs=[],dat=[];
  for(var i=0;i<Math.min((arr||[]).length,12);i++){
    if(arr[i]!==null&&arr[i]!==undefined){
      lbs.push(hdrs&&hdrs[i]?hdrs[i].replace(/-\d{2,4}$/,'').trim():ML[i]);
      dat.push(arr[i]);
    }
  }
  return{labels:lbs,data:dat};
}
function infoItem(lbl,val){ return val&&String(val).trim()&&val!=='—'?'<div class="info-item"><div class="info-lbl">'+lbl+'</div><div class="info-val">'+esc(String(val))+'</div></div>':''; }
function infoItemF(lbl,val){ return'<div class="info-item"><div class="info-lbl">'+lbl+'</div><div class="info-val">'+(val?esc(String(val)):'—')+'</div></div>'; }
function esc(s){ return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }
function escAttr(s){ return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }
function fmtNum(v){
  if(v===null||v===undefined||v==='') return v;
  var n=parseFloat(v); if(isNaN(n)) return v;
  var s=n.toFixed(2); return s.replace(/\.00$/,'');
}

// ══ MODES ═════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function setMode(m){
  viewMode=m;
  document.getElementById('btnYtd').classList.toggle('on',m==='ytd');
  document.getElementById('btnMois').classList.toggle('on',m==='mois');
  if(D){updateC1();updateC2();}
}
function setPyrMode(m){
  pyrMode=m;
  document.getElementById('pyrYB').classList.toggle('on',m==='ytd');
  document.getElementById('pyrMB').classList.toggle('on',m==='mois');
  document.getElementById('pyrSel').style.display=m==='mois'?'inline-block':'none';
  renderPyramid();
}

// ══ PYRAMIDE ══════════════════════════════════════════════════
function getCSSVar(name){ return getComputedStyle(document.documentElement).getPropertyValue(name).trim(); }
function populatePyrMonths(){
  var sel=document.getElementById('pyrSel');
  if(!sel||!D) return;
  var m=D.metrics, hdrs=D.monthHeaders||[];
  var aMj=m.atM_months||[], aMn=m.atm_months||[], aI=m.inc_months||[], aT=m.tags_months||[];
  var n=Math.max(hdrs.length, aMj.length, aMn.length, aI.length, aT.length, 12);
  var prev=sel.value;
  var opts='', firstVal=null, lastVal=null, hasPrev=false;
  for(var i=0;i<n;i++){
    var hasData=(aMj[i]!=null)||(aMn[i]!=null)||(aI[i]!=null)||(aT[i]!=null);
    if(!hasData) continue;
    var lbl=(hdrs[i]?String(hdrs[i]).replace(/-\d{2,4}$/,'').trim():'')||ML[i]||('M'+(i+1));
    var v=String(i);
    opts+='<option value="'+v+'">'+esc(lbl)+'</option>';
    if(firstVal===null) firstVal=v;
    lastVal=v;
    if(v===prev) hasPrev=true;
  }
  sel.innerHTML=opts;
  if(hasPrev) sel.value=prev;
  else if(lastVal!==null) sel.value=lastVal;
}
function renderPyramid(){
  if(!D) return;
  var m=D.metrics;
  populatePyrMonths();
  var sel=document.getElementById('pyrSel');
  var fatal,majeur,mineur,incident,tags;
  if(pyrMode==='ytd'){ fatal=m.at_fatal;majeur=m.at_majeur;mineur=m.at_mineur;incident=m.inc_ytd;tags=m.tags_ytd; }
  else{
    var idx=parseInt(sel&&sel.value,10);
    if(isNaN(idx)){
      // Aucun mois disponible : on bascule sur YTD
      fatal=m.at_fatal;majeur=m.at_majeur;mineur=m.at_mineur;incident=m.inc_ytd;tags=m.tags_ytd;
    } else {
      var aMj=m.atM_months||[], aMn=m.atm_months||[], aI=m.inc_months||[], aT=m.tags_months||[];
      fatal=0;
      majeur  = aMj[idx]!=null ? aMj[idx] : 0;
      mineur  = aMn[idx]!=null ? aMn[idx] : 0;
      incident= aI[idx] !=null ? aI[idx]  : 0;
      tags    = aT[idx] !=null ? aT[idx]  : 0;
    }
  }
  var W=[44,82,126,172,216];
  var cc=['--pyr-conn1','--pyr-conn2','--pyr-conn3','--pyr-conn4'].map(function(v){return getCSSVar(v)||'#333';});
  var legC=['--pyr1b','--pyr2b','--pyr3b','--pyr4b','--pyr5b'].map(function(v){return getCSSVar(v)||'#555';});
  var lv=[{l:'FATAL',i:'💀',v:fatal,c:'pL1',w:W[0]},{l:'MAJEUR',i:'🔴',v:majeur,c:'pL2',w:W[1]},
          {l:'MINEUR',i:'🟠',v:mineur,c:'pL3',w:W[2]},{l:'INCIDENTS',i:'🔵',v:incident,c:'pL4',w:W[3]},
          {l:'TAGs',i:'🟢',v:tags,c:'pL5',w:W[4]}];
  var html='<div class="pyr-outer"><div class="pyr-levels">';
  lv.forEach(function(l,idx){
    if(idx>0){
      var wc=W[idx],df=Math.round((wc-W[idx-1])/2);
      html+='<div class="pyr-conn" style="width:'+wc+'px;margin:0 auto">'
        +'<svg width="'+wc+'" height="5"><polygon points="'+df+',0 '+(wc-df)+',0 '+wc+',5 0,5" fill="'+cc[idx-1]+'"/></svg></div>';
    }
    html+='<div style="display:flex;justify-content:center;width:216px;margin:0 auto">'
      +'<div class="pyr-block '+l.c+'" style="width:'+l.w+'px;height:30px">'
      +'<span class="pi">'+l.i+'</span><span class="pn">'+l.l+'</span><span class="pv">'+fmtNum(l.v)+'</span>'
      +'</div></div>';
  });
  html+='</div><div class="pyr-leg">';
  ['Fatal','Majeur','Mineur','Incident','TAG'].forEach(function(n,i){
    html+='<div class="pyr-li"><div class="pyr-ld" style="background:'+legC[i]+'"></div>'+n+'</div>';
  });
  html+='</div></div>';
  document.getElementById('pyrBox').innerHTML=html;
}

// ══ GRAPHIQUES ════════════════════════════════════════════════
function getCD(sel,m,hdrs){
  var map={
    at:{t:'Accidents AT',sp:'at'},
    tf1:{t:'TF1',c:C.amber,arr:m.tf1_months,ytd:m.tf1_ytd,obj:30,lower:true},
    tg: {t:'TG',c:C.red,  arr:m.tg_months, ytd:m.tg_ytd, obj:0.8,lower:true},
    tvm:{t:'TVM %',c:C.p3,arr:m.tvm_months,ytd:m.tvm,    obj:95, lower:false},
    inc:{t:'Incidents',c:C.purple,arr:m.inc_months,ytd:m.inc_ytd},
    tags:{t:'TAGs',c:C.green,arr:m.tags_months,ytd:m.tags_ytd},
    pres:{t:'Prestataires %',c:C.teal,arr:m.pres_months,ytd:m.prestataires,obj:95,lower:false},
    relt:{t:'Ratio ELT',c:C.amber,arr:m.relt_months,ytd:m.ratio_elt_ytd,obj:350,lower:true},
    rgaz:{t:'Ratio GAZ',c:C.red,  arr:m.rgaz_months,ytd:m.ratio_gaz_ytd,obj:1200,lower:true},
    reau:{t:'Ratio EAU',c:C.p3,   arr:m.reau_months,ytd:m.ratio_eau_ytd,obj:5,lower:true}
  };
  return map[sel]||map.tf1;
}
function drawChart(cid,tid,sel,m,hdrs){
  var dat=getCD(sel,m,hdrs);
  document.getElementById(tid).textContent=dat.t;
  if(dat.sp==='at'){
    var mj=m.atM_months||[], mn=m.atm_months||[];
    var lbs=[],mjD=[],mnD=[];
    for(var i=0;i<Math.max(mj.length,mn.length);i++){
      if(mj[i]!==null||mn[i]!==null){
        lbs.push(hdrs&&hdrs[i]?hdrs[i].replace(/-\d{2,4}$/,'').trim():ML[i]);
        mjD.push(mj[i]||0); mnD.push(mn[i]||0);
      }
    }
    if(viewMode==='ytd'){lbs.push('YTD');mjD.push(m.at_majeur);mnD.push(m.at_mineur);}
    mkChart(cid,'bar',lbs,
      [{label:'Majeur',data:mjD,backgroundColor:'rgba(245,166,35,.85)',borderRadius:4},
       {label:'Mineur',data:mnD,backgroundColor:'rgba(9,99,126,.7)',borderRadius:4}],
      Object.assign({},BASE,{plugins:{legend:{display:true,labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:10},boxWidth:10}}},
        scales:{x:{stacked:true,grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},
                y:{stacked:true,grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt,stepSize:1}}}}));
  } else {
    var cd=cleanMonths(dat.arr||[],hdrs);
    if(viewMode==='ytd'&&dat.ytd!=null){ cd.labels.push('YTD'); cd.data.push(dat.ytd); }
    var ds=[{label:dat.t,data:cd.data,borderColor:dat.c,backgroundColor:dat.c+'22',fill:true,tension:.4,borderWidth:2.5,pointRadius:4,pointBackgroundColor:dat.c}];
    if(dat.obj) ds.push({label:'Obj.',data:cd.labels.map(function(){return dat.obj;}),borderColor:'rgba(232,68,90,.5)',borderDash:[5,4],borderWidth:1.5,pointRadius:0});
    mkChart(cid,'line',cd.labels,ds,Object.assign({},BASE,{plugins:{legend:{display:true,labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:10},boxWidth:10}}}}));
  }
}
function updateC1(){ if(D) drawChart('c1','tC1',document.getElementById('selC1').value,D.metrics,D.monthHeaders); }
function updateC2(){ if(D) drawChart('c2','tC2',document.getElementById('selC2').value,D.metrics,D.monthHeaders); }

// ══ MODAL INCIDENT ════════════════════════════════════════════
function parse5M(text){
  var r={MO:'',MAT:'',METH:'',MIL:'',MGMT:''};
  if(!text) return r;
  var lines=text.split('\n'),curKey=null,cur=[];
  var map=[{keys:["main d'oeuvre","main-d'oeuvre","main d'œuvre","main :"],k:'MO'},
    {keys:['matière','matéri','matériel'],k:'MAT'},{keys:['méthode','methode'],k:'METH'},
    {keys:['milieu','environnement'],k:'MIL'},{keys:['management','machine','mesure'],k:'MGMT'}];
  lines.forEach(function(l){
    var lo=l.toLowerCase().replace(/[*#\\]/g,'').trim(),found=null;
    for(var i=0;i<map.length;i++){for(var j=0;j<map[i].keys.length;j++){if(lo.indexOf(map[i].keys[j])>-1){found=map[i].k;break;}}if(found)break;}
    if(found){if(curKey)r[curKey]=cur.join(' ').trim();curKey=found;cur=[l.replace(/^[-•*#\\: ]+/,'').trim()];}
    else if(curKey&&l.trim()) cur.push(l.replace(/^[-•*#\\ ]+/,'').trim());
  });
  if(curKey) r[curKey]=cur.join(' ').trim();
  return r;
}
function openIncModal(inc){
  var sev=String(inc.gravite||1);
  var sevBg={1:'rgba(9,99,126,.25)',2:'rgba(245,166,35,.2)',3:'rgba(232,68,90,.2)'};
  var sevIco={1:'🔵',2:'🟡',3:'🔴'};
  var badge=document.getElementById('mIncBadge');
  badge.textContent=sevIco[sev]||'⚠️';badge.style.background=sevBg[sev]||sevBg[1];
  badge.style.borderColor=sev==='3'?'var(--red)':sev==='2'?'var(--amber)':'var(--p3)';
  document.getElementById('mIncId').textContent='INC-'+inc.id+(inc.date?' · '+inc.date:'')+(inc.heure?' · '+inc.heure:'');
  document.getElementById('mIncVic').textContent=inc.victime||'Victime non renseignée';
  var chips='<span class="modal-chip">Gravité '+sev+'</span>';
  if(inc.type) chips+='<span class="modal-chip">'+esc(inc.type)+'</span>';
  if(inc.lieu) chips+='<span class="modal-chip">📍 '+esc(inc.lieu)+'</span>';
  if(inc.statut) chips+='<span class="modal-chip" style="color:'+(inc.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('clôt')>-1?'var(--green)':'var(--amber)')+'">'+esc(inc.statut)+'</span>';
  document.getElementById('mIncChips').innerHTML=chips;
  document.getElementById('mIncInfoGrid').innerHTML=[
    infoItemF('Date & Heure',(inc.date||'')+(inc.heure?' à '+inc.heure:'')),
    infoItemF('Lieu / Zone',inc.lieu||'—'),infoItemF('Type',inc.type||'—'),
    infoItemF('Gravité','Niveau '+sev),infoItem('Responsable',inc.responsable),
    infoItem('Délai',inc.delai),infoItemF('Statut',inc.statut||'—')
  ].join('');
  var desc=cleanMd(inc.description||''),dSec=document.getElementById('mIncDescSec');
  if(desc){document.getElementById('mIncDesc').textContent=desc;dSec.style.display='block';}else dSec.style.display='none';
  var causes=cleanMd(inc.causes||''),cSec=document.getElementById('mIncCauseSec');
  if(causes){document.getElementById('mIncCauses').textContent=causes;cSec.style.display='block';}else cSec.style.display='none';
  var m5=parse5M(cleanMd(inc.analyse5m||inc.causes||''));
  var m5Def=[{key:'MO',lbl:"Main-d'œuvre",ico:'👷',cls:'m5-mo',col:'var(--amber)'},
    {key:'MAT',lbl:'Matière/Matériel',ico:'📦',cls:'m5-mat',col:'var(--p3)'},
    {key:'METH',lbl:'Méthode',ico:'📋',cls:'m5-meth',col:'#14b8a6'},
    {key:'MIL',lbl:'Milieu/Env.',ico:'🏭',cls:'m5-mil',col:'var(--green)'},
    {key:'MGMT',lbl:'Machine/Management',ico:'⚙️',cls:'m5-mgmt',col:'#8b5cf6'}];
  document.getElementById('mIncM5').innerHTML=m5Def.map(function(d){
    return'<div class="m5-card '+d.cls+'"><div class="m5-title" style="color:'+d.col+'"><span>'+d.ico+'</span>'+d.lbl+'</div><div class="m5-val">'+(m5[d.key]||'Non renseigné')+'</div></div>';
  }).join('');
  var acts=cleanMd(inc.actions||'');
  var actLines=acts.split('\n').filter(function(l){return l.replace(/[-•*# ]/g,'').trim().length>5;});
  document.getElementById('mIncActions').innerHTML=actLines.length
    ?actLines.map(function(l,i){return'<div class="act-item"><div class="act-num">'+(i+1)+'</div>'+esc(l.replace(/^[-•*#\\ ]+/,'').trim())+'</div>';}).join('')
    :'<div class="info-item"><div class="info-val" style="color:var(--text3)">Actions non renseignées</div></div>';
  document.getElementById('mIncResp').textContent=inc.responsable||'—';
  document.getElementById('mIncDelai').textContent=inc.delai||'—';
  document.getElementById('mIncStatut').textContent=inc.statut||'—';
  document.getElementById('mIncDate2').textContent=inc.date||'—';
  // — Rapport d'enquête (iframe inline, sans quitter le dashboard) —
  (function(){
    var sec   = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteSec');
    var wrap  = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteWrap');
    var empty = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteEmpty');
    var frame = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteFrame');
    var load  = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteLoading');
    var link  = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteNewTab');
    var name  = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteName');
    var btn   = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteExpand');
    var raw   = (inc && inc.enqueteUrl) ? String(inc.enqueteUrl).trim() : '';
    if (!sec) return;
    // Réinitialisation
    if (frame) frame.src = 'about:blank';
    if (load)  load.classList.remove('hide');
    if (!raw || !/^https?:\/\//i.test(raw)) {
      sec.style.display = 'block';
      if (wrap)  wrap.style.display  = 'none';
      if (empty) empty.style.display = 'block';
      if (btn)   btn.style.display   = 'none';
      if (link)  { link.removeAttribute('href'); link.style.display = 'none'; }
      window._mIncEnqueteUrl = '';
      return;
    }
    sec.style.display = 'block';
    if (wrap)  wrap.style.display  = 'flex';
    if (empty) empty.style.display = 'none';
    if (btn)   btn.style.display   = 'inline-flex';
    if (link)  { link.style.display = 'inline-flex'; link.href = raw; }
    if (name)  { name.textContent = 'Rapport d\'enquête · INC-' + inc.id; }
    // Mémorisé pour le bouton « Vue élargie »
    window._mIncEnqueteUrl   = raw;
    window._mIncEnqueteTitle = 'Rapport d\'enquête · INC-' + inc.id;
    // Réutilise le convertisseur Google Drive/Docs/Sheets vers /preview
    var embedUrl = (typeof clnToEmbedUrl === 'function') ? clnToEmbedUrl(raw) : raw;
    if (frame) {
      frame.onload = function(){ if (load) load.classList.add('hide'); };
      frame.src = embedUrl;
    }
  })();
  switchTab('mInc','info',document.querySelector('#incModal .modal-tab'));
  openModal('incModal');
}
// Bouton « Vue élargie » : ouvre le rapport dans le modal embed plein écran
function openIncEnqueteLarge(){
  var url   = window._mIncEnqueteUrl   || '';
  var title = window._mIncEnqueteTitle || "Rapport d'enquête";
  if (!url) return;
  if (typeof openCleaningEmbed === 'function') {
    openCleaningEmbed(url, title, "RAPPORT D'ENQUÊTE", '📑');
  }
}

// ══ MODAL ACCIDENT ════════════════════════════════════════════
function openAccModal(acc){
  document.getElementById('mAccId').textContent=(acc.mois?acc.mois+' · ':'')+acc.date;
  document.getElementById('mAccNom').textContent=acc.nom||'—';
  var chips='<span class="modal-chip">'+esc(acc.mois)+'</span>';
  if(acc.njp>0) chips+='<span class="modal-chip" style="color:var(--red)">NJP : '+acc.njp+' jours</span>';
  if(acc.structure) chips+='<span class="modal-chip">'+esc(acc.structure)+'</span>';
  document.getElementById('mAccChips').innerHTML=chips;
  document.getElementById('mAccInfoGrid').innerHTML=[
    infoItemF('Date',acc.date),infoItemF('Nom',acc.nom),
    infoItemF('Fonction',acc.fonction||'—'),infoItem('Structure',acc.structure),
    infoItemF('Lieu',acc.lieu||'—'),infoItemF('Siège de lésion',acc.siege||'—'),
    infoItemF('Nature de lésion',acc.nature||'—'),infoItemF('Jours Perdus',acc.njp+' jours')
  ].join('');
  var circSec=document.getElementById('mAccCircSec');
  if(acc.circonstance){document.getElementById('mAccCirc').textContent=acc.circonstance;circSec.style.display='block';}else circSec.style.display='none';
  var causeSec=document.getElementById('mAccCauseSec');
  if(acc.cause){document.getElementById('mAccCause').textContent=acc.cause;causeSec.style.display='block';}else causeSec.style.display='none';
  openModal('accModal');
}

// ══ MODAL TAG — Photo Drive automatique ═══════════════════════
// photoRef = nom propre du fichier (sans "tags/")
// photoUrl = URL Drive résolue par le serveur
function openTagModal(tag) {
  document.getElementById('mTagId').textContent  = 'TAG ' + tag.id + (tag.date ? ' · ' + tag.date : '');
  document.getElementById('mTagDesc').textContent = tag.description || '—';
  var isOpen = tag.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('ouvert') > -1 || tag.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('open') > -1;

  var chips = '';
  if (tag.type)        chips += '<span class="modal-chip">'+ esc(tag.type) +'</span>';
  if (tag.gravite)     chips += '<span class="modal-chip">'+ esc(tag.gravite) +'</span>';
  chips += '<span class="modal-chip" style="color:'+(isOpen?'var(--red)':'var(--green)')+'">'+esc(tag.statut)+'</span>';
  if (tag.responsable) chips += '<span class="modal-chip">👤 '+esc(tag.responsable)+'</span>';
  if (tag.hasPhoto)    chips += '<span class="modal-chip" style="color:var(--green)">📸 Drive</span>';
  document.getElementById('mTagChips').innerHTML = chips;

  document.getElementById('mTagInfoGrid').innerHTML = [
    infoItemF('Date création', tag.date),
    infoItem('Date cible', tag.dateCible),
    infoItemF('Type', tag.type||'—'),
    infoItem('Gravité', tag.gravite),
    infoItemF('Zone', (tag.zone||tag.emplacement)||'—'),
    infoItemF('Responsable', tag.responsable||'—'),
    infoItemF('Statut', tag.statut),
    infoItemF('Réf. photo', tag.photoClean||tag.photoRef||'—')
  ].join('');

  var rSec=document.getElementById('mTagRisqueSec');
  if(tag.risque){document.getElementById('mTagRisque').textContent=tag.risque;rSec.style.display='block';}else rSec.style.display='none';
  var aSec=document.getElementById('mTagActionSec');
  if(tag.action){document.getElementById('mTagAction').textContent=tag.action;aSec.style.display='block';}else aSec.style.display='none';
  var pSec=document.getElementById('mTagPropSec');
  if(tag.propositions){document.getElementById('mTagProp').textContent=tag.propositions;pSec.style.display='block';}else pSec.style.display='none';

  // ── PHOTO VIA PROXY BASE64 — AVANT + APRÈS ──────────────
  var photoArea   = document.getElementById('mTagPhotoArea');
  var photoTabBtn = document.getElementById('photoTabBtn');

  var hasAvant = !!(tag.hasPhotoAvant && tag.driveFileIdAvant);
  var hasApres = !!(tag.hasPhotoApres && tag.driveFileIdApres);
  var hasAny   = hasAvant || hasApres;

  if (hasAny) {
    if (photoTabBtn) photoTabBtn.textContent = '📸 Photo Drive';

    // Loader pendant le chargement
    photoArea.innerHTML =
      '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:14px;padding:48px 20px">' +
      '<div class="spin"></div>' +
      '<p style="color:var(--text3);font-size:12px">Chargement depuis Google Drive…</p>' +
      '</div>';

    // Compteur pour savoir quand les deux (ou une seule) photos sont chargées
    var photoResults = { avant: null, apres: null };
    var photosExpected = (hasAvant ? 1 : 0) + (hasApres ? 1 : 0);
    var photosLoaded = 0;

    function renderPhotos() {
      var html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:16px;justify-content:center;width:100%">';

      // Photo AVANT
      if (hasAvant) {
        html += '<div style="flex:1;min-width:220px;max-width:48%;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:6px">';
        html += '<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--amber);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;padding:3px 10px;background:rgba(245,166,35,.12);border:1px solid rgba(245,166,35,.3);border-radius:6px">⚠️ Avant</div>';
        if (photoResults.avant) {
          html += '<img src="'+photoResults.avant+'" style="max-width:100%;max-height:44vh;border-radius:10px;object-fit:contain;border:1px solid var(--border)">';
        } else {
          html += '<div class="photo-noimg" style="padding:16px"><div style="font-size:28px;margin-bottom:6px">⚠️</div><p style="color:var(--amber);font-size:11px">Lecture impossible</p></div>';
        }
        html += '<p style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3)">📁 '+esc(tag.photoClean||tag.photoRef||'—')+'</p>';
        html += '</div>';
      }

      // Photo APRÈS
      if (hasApres) {
        html += '<div style="flex:1;min-width:220px;max-width:48%;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:6px">';
        html += '<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--green);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;padding:3px 10px;background:rgba(16,201,133,.12);border:1px solid rgba(16,201,133,.3);border-radius:6px">✅ Après</div>';
        if (photoResults.apres) {
          html += '<img src="'+photoResults.apres+'" style="max-width:100%;max-height:44vh;border-radius:10px;object-fit:contain;border:1px solid var(--border)">';
        } else {
          html += '<div class="photo-noimg" style="padding:16px"><div style="font-size:28px;margin-bottom:6px">⚠️</div><p style="color:var(--amber);font-size:11px">Lecture impossible</p></div>';
        }
        html += '<p style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3)">📁 '+esc(tag.photoCleanApres||tag.photoRefApres||'après')+'</p>';
        html += '</div>';
      }

      html += '</div>';

      // Barre infos
      html += '<div style="width:100%;background:var(--bg4);border-radius:8px;padding:8px 12px;margin-top:8px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;flex-wrap:wrap">';
      html += '<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">🏷️ TAG '+esc(tag.id)+'</span>';
      if (hasAvant) html += '<span style="font-size:9px;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:4px;background:rgba(245,166,35,.12);color:var(--amber)">Avant ✓</span>';
      if (hasApres) html += '<span style="font-size:9px;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:4px;background:rgba(16,201,133,.12);color:var(--green)">Après ✓</span>';
      if (!hasApres && hasAvant) html += '<span style="font-size:9px;padding:2px 7px;border-radius:4px;background:rgba(232,68,90,.12);color:var(--red)">Après : non disponible</span>';
      html += '</div>';

      photoArea.innerHTML = html;
    }

    function onPhotoLoaded() {
      photosLoaded++;
      if (photosLoaded >= photosExpected) renderPhotos();
    }

    // Charger photo AVANT
    if (hasAvant) {
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(dataUrl) {
          photoResults.avant = dataUrl || null;
          onPhotoLoaded();
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
          photoResults.avant = null;
          onPhotoLoaded();
        })
        .getTagPhotoForClient(tag.driveFileIdAvant);
    }

    // Charger photo APRÈS
    if (hasApres) {
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(dataUrl) {
          photoResults.apres = dataUrl || null;
          onPhotoLoaded();
        })
        .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
          photoResults.apres = null;
          onPhotoLoaded();
        })
        .getTagPhotoForClient(tag.driveFileIdApres);
    }

  } else {
    if (photoTabBtn) photoTabBtn.textContent = '📷 Photo Drive';
    photoArea.innerHTML =
      '<div class="photo-noimg">' +
      '<div style="font-size:52px;margin-bottom:14px">📷</div>' +
      (tag.photoRef
        ? '<p style="color:var(--text2);margin-bottom:6px">Référence : <strong style="color:var(--p4)">' + esc(tag.photoClean||tag.photoRef) + '</strong></p>' +
          '<p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text3);margin-top:8px">Numéro recherché dans Drive : <strong>' +
          esc(((tag.photoClean||'').match(/(\d+)/)||['?'])[0]) + '</strong><br>Fichier non trouvé dans le dossier Tags.</p>'
        : '<p style="color:var(--text3)">Aucune référence photo.</p>') +
      '</div>';
  }

  switchTab('mTag', 'info', document.querySelector('#tagModal .modal-tab'));
  openModal('tagModal');
}

// ══ FILTRES INCIDENTS ═════════════════════════════════════════
function onIncPer(){
  var p=document.getElementById('incPer').value;
  document.getElementById('incMo').style.display=p==='month'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('incYr').style.display=p==='month'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('incD1').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('incSep').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('incD2').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  applyIncF();
}
function applyIncF(){
  if(!D) return;
  var p=document.getElementById('incPer').value;
  var mo=parseInt(document.getElementById('incMo').value)||4;
  var yr=parseInt(document.getElementById('incYr').value)||2026;
  var d1=document.getElementById('incD1').value,d2=document.getElementById('incD2').value;
  var filtered=(D.incidents||[]).filter(function(inc){
    if(!inc.id||inc._err) return false;
    if(!inc.victime&&!inc.description) return false;
    if(p==='all') return true;
    var iso=inc.isoDate; if(!iso) return p==='ytd';
    if(p==='ytd'){ var y=parseInt(iso.substring(0,4)); return y===2026||y===2025; }
    if(p==='month'){ var pts=iso.split('-'); return parseInt(pts[0])===yr&&parseInt(pts[1])===mo; }
    if(p==='custom'){ var ok=true; if(d1)ok=ok&&iso>=d1; if(d2)ok=ok&&iso<=d2; return ok; }
    return true;
  });
  renderIncidents(filtered);
}
function renderIncidents(incs){
  document.getElementById('incStat').textContent=incs.length+' incidents';
  var s3=incs.filter(function(i){return String(i.gravite)==='3';}).length;
  var s2=incs.filter(function(i){return String(i.gravite)==='2';}).length;
  var s1=incs.filter(function(i){return String(i.gravite)==='1';}).length;
  var cl=incs.filter(function(i){return i.statut&&i.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('clôt')>-1;}).length;
  document.getElementById('incKpi').innerHTML=[
    kpiCard('Total',incs.length,'r','incidents','k-r',null,null),
    kpiCard('Grave G3',s3,'r','Gravité 3','k-r',null,null),
    kpiCard('Modéré G2',s2,'a','Gravité 2','k-a',null,null),
    kpiCard('Faible G1',s1,'b','Gravité 1','k-b',null,null),
    kpiCard('Clôturés',cl,'g','soldés','k-g',null,null)
  ].join('');
  // Zones
  var zones={};
  incs.forEach(function(i){if(i.lieu){var z=i.lieu.substring(0,25);zones[z]=(zones[z]||0)+1;}});
  var zk=Object.keys(zones).sort(function(a,b){return zones[b]-zones[a];}).slice(0,5);
  mkChart('zoneC','bar',zk,[{data:zk.map(function(k){return zones[k];}),backgroundColor:[C.red,C.amber,C.p2,C.teal,C.purple],borderRadius:5}],
    Object.assign({},BASE,{indexAxis:'y',scales:{x:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},y:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9}}}}}));
  // Causes racines (statique)
  document.getElementById('causeGrid').innerHTML=[
    ['Sol mouillé / glissade'],['Bords tranchants / carton'],['Chute d\'objet / palette'],
    ['Mauvaise méthode'],['Manque vigilance'],['Collision engin']
  ].map(function(c,i){
    return'<div style="background:var(--bg3);border-radius:7px;padding:8px 10px;transition:background .3s">'
      +'<div style="font-size:17px;font-weight:800;font-family:\'JetBrains Mono\',monospace;color:var(--amber);margin-bottom:1px">'+(6-i)+'</div>'
      +'<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text3)">'+c[0]+'</div></div>';
  }).join('');
  // Liste
  var il=document.getElementById('incList'); il.innerHTML='';
  if(incs.length===0){il.innerHTML='<div style="padding:16px;text-align:center;color:var(--text3);font-size:12px">Aucun incident pour cette période</div>';return;}
  incs.forEach(function(inc){
    if(!inc.id||inc._err) return;
    var sev=String(inc.gravite||1);
    var stat=(inc.statut||'').toLowerCase().indexOf('clôt')>-1?'Clôturé':'En cours';
    var el=document.createElement('div');
    el.className='iitem is'+sev; el.tabIndex=0;
    el.innerHTML='<div class="ihdr"><span class="iid">INC-'+esc(inc.id)+(inc.date?' · '+inc.date:'')+'</span><span class="isev sv'+sev+'">G'+sev+'</span></div>'
      +'<div class="ivic">'+(inc.victime||'—')+'</div>'
      +(inc.description?'<div class="idesc">'+esc(inc.description.substring(0,90))+(inc.description.length>90?'…':'')+'</div>':'')
      +'<div class="itags">'+(inc.lieu?'<span class="itag">📍 '+esc(inc.lieu)+'</span>':'')+(inc.type?'<span class="itag">'+esc(inc.type)+'</span>':'')
      +'<span class="'+(stat==='Clôturé'?'s-close':'s-open')+'">'+stat+'</span>'
      +'<span class="iclick-hint">🔍 Voir détails</span></div>';
    el.onclick=function(){openIncModal(inc);};
    el.onkeydown=function(e){if(e.key==='Enter'||e.key===' ')openIncModal(inc);};
    il.appendChild(el);
  });
}

// ══ FILTRES TAGS ══════════════════════════════════════════════
function populateTagDropdowns(){
  if(!D||!D.tags) return;
  var resps=new Set(),zones=new Set();
  D.tags.forEach(function(t){
    if(t.responsable&&t.responsable.trim()) resps.add(t.responsable.trim());
    var z=(t.zone||t.emplacement||'').trim(); if(z) zones.add(z);
  });
  var rSel=document.getElementById('tagFilterResp');
  rSel.innerHTML='<option value="all">Tous ('+resps.size+')</option>';
  Array.from(resps).sort().forEach(function(r){rSel.innerHTML+='<option value="'+esc(r)+'">'+esc(r)+'</option>';});
  var zSel=document.getElementById('tagFilterZone');
  zSel.innerHTML='<option value="all">Toutes ('+zones.size+')</option>';
  Array.from(zones).sort().forEach(function(z){zSel.innerHTML+='<option value="'+esc(z)+'">'+esc(z)+'</option>';});
}
function setTagStat(val,el){
  tagStatFilter=val;
  document.querySelectorAll('#tagStatChips .tag-filter-chip').forEach(function(c){c.classList.remove('on');});
  el.classList.add('on');
  applyTagF();
}
function onTagPer(){
  var p=document.getElementById('tagPer').value;
  document.getElementById('tagYr').style.display=p==='month'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('tagMo').style.display=p==='month'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('tagD1').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('tagSep').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('tagD2').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  applyTagF();
}
function clearTagFilters(){
  document.getElementById('tagSearch').value='';
  document.getElementById('tagSort').value='date_desc';
  document.getElementById('tagPer').value='all';
  ['tagYr','tagMo','tagD1','tagSep','tagD2'].forEach(function(id){document.getElementById(id).style.display='none';});
  document.getElementById('tagFilterResp').value='all';
  document.getElementById('tagFilterZone').value='all';
  tagStatFilter='all';
  document.querySelectorAll('#tagStatChips .tag-filter-chip').forEach(function(c,i){c.classList.toggle('on',i===0);});
  applyTagF();
}
function applyTagF(){
  if(!D) return;
  var p=document.getElementById('tagPer').value;
  var yr=parseInt(document.getElementById('tagYr').value)||2026;
  var mo=parseInt(document.getElementById('tagMo').value)||1;
  var d1=document.getElementById('tagD1').value,d2=document.getElementById('tagD2').value;
  var searchVal=(document.getElementById('tagSearch').value||'').toLowerCase().trim();
  var sortVal=document.getElementById('tagSort').value;
  var filterResp=document.getElementById('tagFilterResp').value;
  var filterZone=document.getElementById('tagFilterZone').value;

  var filtered=(D.tags||[]).filter(function(t){
    if(!t.id||t._err) return false;
    var isOpen=t.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('ouvert')>-1||t.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('open')>-1;
    if(tagStatFilter==='open'&&!isOpen) return false;
    if(tagStatFilter==='closed'&&isOpen) return false;
    if(filterResp!=='all'&&(t.responsable||'').trim()!==filterResp) return false;
    if(filterZone!=='all'){var z=(t.zone||t.emplacement||'').trim();if(z!==filterZone)return false;}
    if(p!=='all'){
      if(!t.isoDate) return p==='ytd';
      var pts=t.isoDate.split('-');
      if(p==='ytd'&&parseInt(pts[0])!==2026) return false;
      if(p==='month'&&(parseInt(pts[0])!==yr||parseInt(pts[1])!==mo)) return false;
      if(p==='custom'){if(d1&&t.isoDate<d1)return false;if(d2&&t.isoDate>d2)return false;}
    }
    if(searchVal){
      // Recherche dans tous les champs, SAUF "tag" et "tags" ignorés
      var hay=(t.description+' '+(t.zone||t.emplacement||'')+' '+t.type+' '
        +t.responsable+' '+t.id+' '+t.risque+' '
        // photoRef sans "tag" ni "tags"
        +(t.photoRef||'').replace(/\btags?\b/gi,'')).toLowerCase();
      if(hay.indexOf(searchVal)===-1) return false;
    }
    return true;
  });

  // Tri
  filtered.sort(function(a,b){
    if(sortVal==='date_desc'){if(!a.isoDate)return 1;if(!b.isoDate)return -1;return b.isoDate.localeCompare(a.isoDate);}
    if(sortVal==='date_asc'){ if(!a.isoDate)return 1;if(!b.isoDate)return -1;return a.isoDate.localeCompare(b.isoDate);}
    if(sortVal==='id_asc')  return String(a.id).localeCompare(String(b.id),undefined,{numeric:true});
    if(sortVal==='id_desc') return String(b.id).localeCompare(String(a.id),undefined,{numeric:true});
    if(sortVal==='zone_az') return (a.zone||a.emplacement||'').localeCompare(b.zone||b.emplacement||'');
    if(sortVal==='resp_az') return (a.responsable||'').localeCompare(b.responsable||'');
    return 0;
  });

  var total=D.tags.length;
  var openAll=D.tagsOpen.length,closedAll=total-openAll;
  var openF=filtered.filter(function(t){return t.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('ouvert')>-1||t.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('open')>-1;}).length;
  var closedF=filtered.length-openF;
  var cloPct=filtered.length>0?Math.round(closedF/filtered.length*100):0;

  document.getElementById('tagStatsRow').innerHTML=
    '<span class="tag-stat-pill tsp-total">Total : '+total+'</span>'
    +'<span class="tag-stat-pill tsp-open">Ouverts : '+openAll+'</span>'
    +'<span class="tag-stat-pill tsp-closed">Fermés : '+closedAll+'</span>'
    +(filtered.length!==total?'<span class="tag-stat-pill tsp-filtered">Filtrés : <strong>'+filtered.length+'</strong></span>':'');
  document.getElementById('tagListCount').textContent=filtered.length+' résultats';

  document.getElementById('tagKpi').innerHTML=[
    kpiCard('Filtrés',filtered.length,'b','TAGs','k-b',null,null),
    kpiCard('Fermés',closedF,'g','✓','k-g',cloPct,C.green),
    kpiCard('Ouverts',openF,'r','⚠','k-r',filtered.length>0?Math.round(openF/filtered.length*100):0,C.red),
    kpiCard('Clôture',fmtNum(cloPct)+'%','g','obj.95%','k-g',cloPct,cloPct>=95?C.green:cloPct>50?C.amber:C.red)
  ].join('');

  // Types de dangers
  var types={};
  filtered.forEach(function(t){if(t.type){var ty=t.type.substring(0,22);types[ty]=(types[ty]||0)+1;}});
  var tk=Object.keys(types).sort(function(a,b){return types[b]-types[a];}).slice(0,6);
  if(charts['dangerC'])charts['dangerC'].destroy();
  if(tk.length>0) new Chart(document.getElementById('dangerC'),{type:'doughnut',
    data:{labels:tk,datasets:[{data:tk.map(function(k){return types[k];}),backgroundColor:[C.amber,C.red,C.p2,C.teal,C.green,C.orange],borderWidth:0,hoverOffset:4}]},
    options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{display:true,position:'right',labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9},boxWidth:8}}},cutout:'50%'}});

  // Zones TAGs
  var tzones={};
  filtered.forEach(function(t){if(t.zone||t.emplacement){var z=(t.zone||t.emplacement).substring(0,18);tzones[z]=(tzones[z]||0)+1;}});
  var tzk=Object.keys(tzones).sort(function(a,b){return tzones[b]-tzones[a];}).slice(0,6);
  mkChart('tagZoneC','bar',tzk,[{data:tzk.map(function(k){return tzones[k];}),backgroundColor:'rgba(9,99,126,.75)',borderRadius:4}],
    Object.assign({},BASE,{indexAxis:'y',scales:{x:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},y:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9}}}}}));

  // Table avec vignettes Avant / Après inline (chargement asynchrone)
  var tb=document.getElementById('tagBody'); tb.innerHTML='';
  if(filtered.length===0){
    var msg=searchVal?'Aucun TAG pour "'+esc(searchVal)+'"'
      :filterResp!=='all'?'Aucun TAG pour "'+esc(filterResp)+'"'
      :filterZone!=='all'?'Aucun TAG zone "'+esc(filterZone)+'"'
      :'Aucun TAG pour ce filtre';
    tb.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="10" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:20px">'+msg+'</td></tr>';
    return;
  }
  function hl(str){
    if(!searchVal||!str) return esc(str||'');
    var re=new RegExp('('+searchVal.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g,'\\$&')+')','gi');
    return esc(str).replace(re,'<mark style="background:rgba(245,166,35,.35);border-radius:2px;padding:0 1px">$1</mark>');
  }
  var pendingTagThumbs=[];
  filtered.forEach(function(t,idx){
    var isOpen=t.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('ouvert')>-1||t.statut.toLowerCase().indexOf('open')>-1;
    var respHtml=t.responsable
      ?'<span class="rbadge" style="color:var(--p4)">'+hl(t.responsable)+'</span>'
      :'<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:9px">—</span>';

    // ── Vignettes Avant / Après — chargement asynchrone via google.script.run
    function tagThumbCell(label, has, fid, ref){
      var cellId='tagThumb_'+idx+'_'+label;
      if(!has||!fid){
        return '<td class="cln-thumb-cell"><div class="cln-thumb-ph" title="Pas de photo '+label+'">📷</div></td>';
      }
      pendingTagThumbs.push({fid:fid,cellId:cellId,label:label,ref:ref||'',tag:t});
      return '<td class="cln-thumb-cell"><div id="'+cellId+'" class="cln-thumb-load" title="Chargement photo '+label+' depuis Drive…"></div></td>';
    }
    // L'ordre des colonnes Avant puis Après est garanti côté HTML
    var avantCellHtml=tagThumbCell('Avant', t.hasPhotoAvant, t.driveFileIdAvant, t.photoClean||t.photoRef);
    var apresCellHtml=tagThumbCell('Après', t.hasPhotoApres, t.driveFileIdApres, t.photoCleanApres||t.photoRefApres||t.photoClean||t.photoRef);

    var tr=document.createElement('tr');
    tr.style.cursor='pointer';
    tr.innerHTML='<td class="mono" style="color:var(--p4)">'+esc(t.id)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="white-space:nowrap;font-size:10px">'+t.date+'</td>'
      +avantCellHtml+apresCellHtml
      +'<td style="font-size:10px;max-width:180px">'+hl(t.description.substring(0,80))+(t.description.length>80?'…':'')+'</td>'
      +'<td><span class="rbadge">'+hl((t.zone||t.emplacement)||'—')+'</span></td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:10px">'+hl(t.type)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="white-space:nowrap;font-size:10px">'+esc(t.dateCible||'—')+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:10px">'+respHtml+'</td>'
      +'<td><span class="'+(isOpen?'s-open':'s-close')+'">'+(isOpen?'Ouvert':'Fermé')+'</span></td>';
    tr.addEventListener('click',function(){ openTagModal(t); });
    tb.appendChild(tr);
  });

  // ── Chargement asynchrone des vignettes (avec cache partagé) ──
  if(!window._tagPhotoCache) window._tagPhotoCache={};
  pendingTagThumbs.forEach(function(p){
    var slot=document.getElementById(p.cellId);
    if(!slot) return;
    var cached=window._tagPhotoCache[p.fid];
    if(cached){ replaceTagThumb(slot,cached,p); return; }
    google.script.run
      .withSuccessHandler(function(d){
        if(d){ window._tagPhotoCache[p.fid]=d; replaceTagThumb(slot,d,p); }
        else if(slot && slot.parentNode){ slot.outerHTML='<div class="cln-thumb-ph" title="Lecture impossible">⚠️</div>'; }
      })
      .withFailureHandler(function(){
        if(slot && slot.parentNode){ slot.outerHTML='<div class="cln-thumb-ph" title="Lecture impossible">⚠️</div>'; }
      })
      .getTagPhotoForClient(p.fid);
  });
}

function replaceTagThumb(slot, dataUrl, p){
  if(!slot||!slot.parentNode) return;
  var img=document.createElement('img');
  img.src=dataUrl;
  img.className='cln-thumb';
  img.alt=p.label;
  img.title=p.label+(p.ref?' · '+p.ref:'')+' (cliquer pour agrandir)';
  img.addEventListener('click',function(e){
    e.stopPropagation();
    openTagModal(p.tag);
    var photoTab=document.querySelectorAll('#tagModal .modal-tab')[1];
    if(photoTab) switchTab('mTag','photo',photoTab);
  });
  slot.parentNode.replaceChild(img,slot);
}

// ══ FILTRES ACCIDENTS ═════════════════════════════════════════
function onAccPer(){
  var p=document.getElementById('accPer').value;
  document.getElementById('accMo').style.display=p==='month'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('accD1').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('accSep').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  document.getElementById('accD2').style.display=p==='custom'?'inline-block':'none';
  applyAccF();
}
function applyAccF(){
  if(!D) return;
  var p=document.getElementById('accPer').value,mois=document.getElementById('accMo').value;
  var d1=document.getElementById('accD1').value,d2=document.getElementById('accD2').value;
  var filtered=(D.accidents||[]).filter(function(a){
    if(!a.nom||a._err||a.nom.length<3) return false;
    if(p==='all') return true; if(p==='ytd') return true;
    if(p==='month') return a.mois===mois;
    if(p==='custom'){if(!a.isoDate)return true;var ok=true;if(d1)ok=ok&&a.isoDate>=d1;if(d2)ok=ok&&a.isoDate<=d2;return ok;}
    return true;
  });
  renderAccidents(filtered);
}
function renderAccidents(accs){
  document.getElementById('accStat').textContent=accs.length+' accidents';
  var totalNJP=0; accs.forEach(function(a){totalNJP+=a.njp;});
  var njpM={Janvier:0,Février:0,Mars:0,Avril:0};
  accs.forEach(function(a){if(njpM[a.mois]!==undefined)njpM[a.mois]+=a.njp;});
  var maxMois=Object.keys(njpM).reduce(function(a,b){return njpM[a]>njpM[b]?a:b;},'Janvier');
  document.getElementById('accCount').textContent=accs.length+' accidents';
  document.getElementById('accSum').innerHTML=
    '<div class="acc-card"><div class="acc-val" style="color:var(--red)">'+fmtNum(accs.length)+'</div><div class="acc-lbl">AT filtrés</div></div>'+
    '<div class="acc-card"><div class="acc-val" style="color:var(--amber)">'+fmtNum(totalNJP)+'</div><div class="acc-lbl">NJP total</div></div>'+
    '<div class="acc-card"><div class="acc-val" style="color:var(--p4)">'+fmtNum(njpM[maxMois])+'</div><div class="acc-lbl">NJP max</div></div>'+
    '<div class="acc-card"><div class="acc-val" style="color:var(--green)">'+maxMois+'</div><div class="acc-lbl">Mois +accid.</div></div>';
  var njpL=[],njpD=[];
  ['Janvier','Février','Mars','Avril'].forEach(function(mo){if(njpM[mo]>=0){njpL.push(mo.substring(0,3));njpD.push(njpM[mo]);}});
  if(njpL.length>0) mkChart('njpC','bar',njpL,[{data:njpD,backgroundColor:[C.red,'rgba(232,68,90,.7)','rgba(232,68,90,.5)','rgba(232,68,90,.4)'],borderRadius:5}],BASE);
  var zones={};accs.forEach(function(a){if(a.lieu){var z=a.lieu.substring(0,25);zones[z]=(zones[z]||0)+1;}});
  var zk=Object.keys(zones).sort(function(a,b){return zones[b]-zones[a];}).slice(0,5);
  if(zk.length>0) mkChart('accZC','bar',zk,[{data:zk.map(function(k){return zones[k];}),backgroundColor:'rgba(9,99,126,.75)',borderRadius:4}],
    Object.assign({},BASE,{indexAxis:'y',scales:{x:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},y:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9}}}}}));
  var causes={};accs.forEach(function(a){if(a.cause){var c=a.cause.substring(0,35);causes[c]=(causes[c]||0)+1;}});
  var ck=Object.keys(causes).sort(function(a,b){return causes[b]-causes[a];}).slice(0,5);
  if(ck.length>0) mkChart('accCC','bar',ck,[{data:ck.map(function(k){return causes[k];}),backgroundColor:[C.amber,C.red,C.p2,C.teal,C.purple],borderRadius:4}],
    Object.assign({},BASE,{indexAxis:'y',scales:{x:{grid:{color:C.grid},ticks:{color:C.txt}},y:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9}}}}}));
  var foncs={};accs.forEach(function(a){if(a.fonction){var f=a.fonction.substring(0,25);foncs[f]=(foncs[f]||0)+1;}});
  var fk=Object.keys(foncs).sort(function(a,b){return foncs[b]-foncs[a];}).slice(0,5);
  if(fk.length>0){if(charts['accFC'])charts['accFC'].destroy();new Chart(document.getElementById('accFC'),{type:'doughnut',
    data:{labels:fk,datasets:[{data:fk.map(function(k){return foncs[k];}),backgroundColor:[C.amber,C.red,C.p2,C.teal,C.green],borderWidth:0,hoverOffset:4}]},
    options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,plugins:{legend:{display:true,position:'right',labels:{color:C.txt,font:{size:9},boxWidth:8}}},cutout:'50%'}});}
  var ab=document.getElementById('accBody'); ab.innerHTML='';
  if(accs.length===0){ab.innerHTML='<tr><td colspan="9" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:16px">Aucun accident</td></tr>';return;}
  accs.forEach(function(a){
    var tr=document.createElement('tr'); tr.className='acc-row'; tr.title='Cliquer pour détails';
    tr.innerHTML='<td><span class="rbadge">'+esc(a.mois)+'</span></td>'
      +'<td class="mono" style="font-size:9px;white-space:nowrap">'+a.date+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-weight:600;color:var(--text)">'+esc(a.nom)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:10px">'+esc(a.fonction)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:10px">'+esc(a.lieu)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:10px">'+esc(a.siege)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:10px">'+esc(a.nature)+'</td>'
      +'<td class="mono" style="color:var(--red);font-weight:700;text-align:center">'+fmtNum(a.njp)+'</td>'
      +'<td style="font-size:10px;max-width:100px">'+esc(a.cause.substring(0,40))+(a.cause.length>40?'…':'')+'</td>';
    tr.addEventListener('click',function(){openAccModal(a);});
    ab.appendChild(tr);
  });
}

// ══ ÉNERGIE ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════
function setEnvMode(m){
  envMode=m;
  document.getElementById('envC').classList.toggle('on',m==='conso');
  document.getElementById('envR').classList.toggle('on',m==='ratio');
  if(D) updateEnvCharts();
}
function updateEnvCharts(){
  var m=D.metrics,isR=envMode==='ratio',hdrs=D.monthHeaders||[];
  document.getElementById('tElt').textContent=isR?'Ratio ELT kWh/UP':'Électricité kWh';
  document.getElementById('tGaz').textContent=isR?'Ratio GAZ m³/UP':'Gaz m³';
  document.getElementById('tEau').textContent=isR?'Ratio EAU m³/UP':'Eau m³';
  var eA=isR?m.relt_months:m.elt_months,gA=isR?m.rgaz_months:m.gaz_months,wA=isR?m.reau_months:m.eau_months;
  var ce=cleanMonths(eA||[],hdrs),cg=cleanMonths(gA||[],hdrs),cw=cleanMonths(wA||[],hdrs);
  mkChart('eltC','line',ce.labels,[{data:ce.data,borderColor:C.amber,backgroundColor:'rgba(245,166,35,.12)',fill:true,tension:.4,borderWidth:2.5,pointRadius:4,pointBackgroundColor:C.amber}],BASE);
  mkChart('gazC','line',cg.labels,[{data:cg.data,borderColor:C.red,backgroundColor:'rgba(232,68,90,.12)',fill:true,tension:.4,borderWidth:2.5,pointRadius:4,pointBackgroundColor:C.red}],BASE);
  mkChart('eauC','bar',cw.labels,[{data:cw.data,backgroundColor:[C.p1,'rgba(9,99,126,.7)','rgba(9,99,126,.5)'],borderRadius:5}],BASE);
}

// ══ NETTOYAGE ═════════════════════════════════════════════════
// État dérivé des photos :
//   - photo « Avant » seule           → en cours
//   - photos « Avant » ET « Après »   → terminé
//   - aucune photo                    → indéfini (ne compte pas)
function clnHasAvant(c){ return !!(c && c.hasPhotoAvant && c.driveFileIdAvant); }
function clnHasApres(c){ return !!(c && c.hasPhotoApres && c.driveFileIdApres); }
function isClnOpen(c){
  return clnHasAvant(c) && !clnHasApres(c);
}
function isClnClosed(c){
  return clnHasAvant(c) && clnHasApres(c);
}
function setClnStat(s,el){
  clnStatFilter = s;
  document.querySelectorAll('#clnStatChips .tag-filter-chip').forEach(function(c){c.classList.remove('on');});
  el.classList.add('on');
  applyClnF();
}

// ── PLAN DE NETTOYAGE ─────────────────────────────────────────
// Lecture dynamique de D.cleaningPlan (issu de la feuille « nettoyage 1 »)
// Affiche 4 zones cibles → ouvre le lien associé dans un nouvel onglet.
var CLN_PLAN_ZONES = [
  { label:'Étage -1',     icon:'🅑' },
  { label:'Étage 0',      icon:'0️⃣' },
  { label:'Étage 1',      icon:'1️⃣' },
  { label:'Voie externe', icon:'🛣️' }
];
function clnPlanNorm(s){
  return String(s||'').toLowerCase()
    .replace(/[éèêë]/g,'e').replace(/[àâä]/g,'a').replace(/[ùûü]/g,'u')
    .replace(/[îï]/g,'i').replace(/[ôö]/g,'o').replace(/[ç]/g,'c')
    .replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();
}
function clnPlanResolveLink(zoneLabel){
  var data = (D && D.cleaningPlan) ? D.cleaningPlan : [];
  if (!data.length) return '';
  var key = clnPlanNorm(zoneLabel);
  // 1) match exact normalisé
  for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (clnPlanNorm(data[i].zone) === key) return data[i].link || '';
  }
  // 2) match « contains » (tolère « Étage -1 » vs « etage -1 - sous-sol », etc.)
  for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    var z = clnPlanNorm(data[i].zone);
    if (z.indexOf(key) > -1 || key.indexOf(z) > -1) return data[i].link || '';
  }
  return '';
}
function openCleaningPlan(){
  var list  = document.getElementById('clnPlanList');
  var empty = document.getElementById('clnPlanEmpty');
  if (!list || !empty) return;

  var data = (D && D.cleaningPlan) ? D.cleaningPlan : [];
  // On considère qu'il y a des données « plan » si au moins une zone a un lien plan
  var hasAnyPlan = data.some(function(d){ return d && d.link; });
  if (!data.length || !hasAnyPlan) {
    list.innerHTML = '';
    list.style.display = 'none';
    empty.style.display = 'block';
    openModal('clnPlanModal');
    return;
  }

  var html = '';
  CLN_PLAN_ZONES.forEach(function(z){
    var link = clnPlanResolveLink(z.label);
    var disabled = !link;
    var safeTitle = esc(z.label);
    html += '<button class="cln-plan-btn'+(disabled?' disabled':'')+'" '
         +  (disabled
              ? 'disabled title="Lien plan non défini dans la feuille nettoyage 1"'
              : 'onclick="openCleaningPlanLink(\''+encodeURIComponent(link)+'\',\''+encodeURIComponent(z.label)+'\')"'
            )
         +  '>'
         +    '<span class="cln-plan-icon">'+z.icon+'</span>'
         +    '<span class="cln-plan-zone">'+safeTitle+'</span>'
         +    '<span class="cln-plan-arrow">'+(disabled?'⛔':'↗')+'</span>'
         +  '</button>';
  });
  list.innerHTML = html;
  list.style.display  = 'grid';
  empty.style.display = 'none';
  openModal('clnPlanModal');
}
function openCleaningPlanLink(encoded, encodedTitle){
  var url = '';
  try { url = decodeURIComponent(encoded || ''); } catch(e) { url = encoded || ''; }
  var title = '';
  try { title = decodeURIComponent(encodedTitle || ''); } catch(e2) { title = encodedTitle || ''; }
  if (!url) return;
  if (!/^https?:\/\//i.test(url)) {
    alert('Lien invalide pour cette zone : ' + url);
    return;
  }
  openCleaningEmbed(url, title || 'Plan de nettoyage', 'PLAN DE NETTOYAGE', '📋');
}

// ── PRODUITS UTILISÉS ────────────────────────────────────────
// Deux formats supportés :
//
// (1) Catalogue GLOBAL (D.cleaningProducts) — sous-tableau
//     « PRODUITS UTILISÉS » avec colonnes Nom de produit | Lien
//     de fiche (FDS). Chaque ligne = un produit. Affiché en
//     priorité s'il existe.
//
// (2) Format PAR ZONE (D.cleaningPlan[i].productsLink/Text) —
//     ancien modèle où chaque zone a son propre lien produits.
//     Utilisé en fallback si le catalogue global est vide.
function clnProductsResolve(zoneLabel){
  var data = (D && D.cleaningPlan) ? D.cleaningPlan : [];
  if (!data.length) return { link:'', text:'' };
  var key = clnPlanNorm(zoneLabel);
  for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (clnPlanNorm(data[i].zone) === key) {
      return { link: data[i].productsLink || '', text: data[i].productsText || '' };
    }
  }
  for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    var z = clnPlanNorm(data[i].zone);
    if (z.indexOf(key) > -1 || key.indexOf(z) > -1) {
      return { link: data[i].productsLink || '', text: data[i].productsText || '' };
    }
  }
  return { link:'', text:'' };
}
function openCleaningProducts(){
  var list  = document.getElementById('clnProductsList');
  var empty = document.getElementById('clnProductsEmpty');
  if (!list || !empty) return;

  // Sous-titre dynamique du modal
  function setSubtitle(text){
    var el = document.querySelector('#clnProductsModal .modal-hdr-name');
    if (el) el.textContent = text;
  }

  // ── Cas 1 : catalogue GLOBAL « PRODUITS UTILISÉS » ────────
  // (sous-tableau Nom de produit | Lien de fiche dans la feuille)
  var products = (D && D.cleaningProducts) ? D.cleaningProducts : [];
  if (products && products.length) {
    var html = '';
    products.forEach(function(p){
      var name = String((p && p.name) || '').trim();
      var link = String((p && p.link) || '').trim();
      var text = String((p && p.text) || '').trim();
      if (!name) return;
      var hasLink = !!link && /^https?:\/\//i.test(link);
      var arrow   = hasLink ? '↗' : '📄';
      var icon    = '🧴';
      var subTxt;
      if (hasLink)      subTxt = 'Voir la fiche (FDS)';
      else if (text)    subTxt = (text.length > 90 ? text.substring(0,90)+'…' : text);
      else              subTxt = 'Aucune fiche renseignée';
      var subSpan = '<span class="cln-plan-sub">'+esc(subTxt)+'</span>';

      if (hasLink) {
        html += '<button class="cln-plan-btn" '
             +  'onclick="openCleaningProductsLink(\''+encodeURIComponent(link)+'\',\''+encodeURIComponent(name)+'\')">'
             +    '<span class="cln-plan-icon">'+icon+'</span>'
             +    '<span class="cln-plan-zone">'+esc(name)+subSpan+'</span>'
             +    '<span class="cln-plan-arrow">'+arrow+'</span>'
             +  '</button>';
      } else {
        html += '<button class="cln-plan-btn disabled" disabled '
             +  'title="'+esc(text || 'Aucune fiche renseignée')+'">'
             +    '<span class="cln-plan-icon">'+icon+'</span>'
             +    '<span class="cln-plan-zone">'+esc(name)+subSpan+'</span>'
             +    '<span class="cln-plan-arrow">'+arrow+'</span>'
             +  '</button>';
      }
    });
    list.innerHTML = html;
    list.style.display  = 'grid';
    empty.style.display = 'none';
    setSubtitle(products.length + ' produit' + (products.length>1?'s':'') + ' référencé' + (products.length>1?'s':''));
    openModal('clnProductsModal');
    return;
  }

  // ── Cas 2 : ancien modèle PAR ZONE (rétro-compatibilité) ──
  var data = (D && D.cleaningPlan) ? D.cleaningPlan : [];
  var anyProducts = data.some(function(d){ return d && (d.productsLink || d.productsText); });

  if (!data.length || !anyProducts) {
    list.innerHTML = '';
    list.style.display = 'none';
    empty.style.display = 'block';
    setSubtitle('Aucun produit trouvé');
    openModal('clnProductsModal');
    return;
  }

  setSubtitle('Sélectionnez une zone');
  var html = '';
  CLN_PLAN_ZONES.forEach(function(z){
    var p = clnProductsResolve(z.label);
    var hasLink = !!p.link;
    var hasText = !!p.text;
    var disabled = !hasLink && !hasText;

    var arrow = disabled ? '⛔' : (hasLink ? '↗' : '📄');
    var safeTitle = esc(z.label);
    var subTxt = '';
    if (hasText) {
      var t = p.text;
      if (t.length > 90) t = t.substring(0,90) + '…';
      subTxt = '<span class="cln-plan-sub">'+esc(t)+'</span>';
    } else if (hasLink) {
      subTxt = '<span class="cln-plan-sub">Voir les produits utilisés</span>';
    } else {
      subTxt = '<span class="cln-plan-sub">Aucun produit renseigné</span>';
    }

    if (hasLink) {
      html += '<button class="cln-plan-btn" '
           +  'onclick="openCleaningProductsLink(\''+encodeURIComponent(p.link)+'\',\''+encodeURIComponent(z.label)+'\')">'
           +    '<span class="cln-plan-icon">'+z.icon+'</span>'
           +    '<span class="cln-plan-zone">'+safeTitle+subTxt+'</span>'
           +    '<span class="cln-plan-arrow">'+arrow+'</span>'
           +  '</button>';
    } else {
      // Pas de lien → bouton informatif (texte seulement)
      html += '<button class="cln-plan-btn'+(disabled?' disabled':'')+'" '
           +  (disabled ? 'disabled' : 'onclick="void 0"')
           +  ' title="'+esc(p.text || 'Aucun produit renseigné')+'">'
           +    '<span class="cln-plan-icon">'+z.icon+'</span>'
           +    '<span class="cln-plan-zone">'+safeTitle+subTxt+'</span>'
           +    '<span class="cln-plan-arrow">'+arrow+'</span>'
           +  '</button>';
    }
  });
  list.innerHTML = html;
  list.style.display  = 'grid';
  empty.style.display = 'none';
  openModal('clnProductsModal');
}
function openCleaningProductsLink(encoded, encodedTitle){
  var url = '';
  try { url = decodeURIComponent(encoded || ''); } catch(e) { url = encoded || ''; }
  var title = '';
  try { title = decodeURIComponent(encodedTitle || ''); } catch(e2) { title = encodedTitle || ''; }
  if (!url) return;
  if (!/^https?:\/\//i.test(url)) {
    alert('Lien invalide pour cette zone : ' + url);
    return;
  }
  openCleaningEmbed(url, title || 'Produits utilisés', 'PRODUITS UTILISÉS', '🧴');
}

// ── EMBED — convertit une URL Google en URL embeddable + ouvre l'iframe modal ──
// Permet d'afficher le contenu DANS le dashboard (pas de redirection externe).
function clnToEmbedUrl(url){
  if (!url) return '';
  try {
    // Google Sheets : /edit?gid=... → /preview?gid=...  (ou /htmlview en fallback)
    var mSheet = url.match(/^(https:\/\/docs\.google\.com\/spreadsheets\/d\/[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)\/(edit|view|htmlview|preview)?(\?[^#]*)?(#.*)?$/i);
    if (mSheet) {
      var base  = mSheet[1];
      var query = mSheet[3] || '';
      var hash  = mSheet[4] || '';
      // Conserve le gid si présent
      var gidMatch = (query + hash).match(/gid=(\d+)/);
      var gidQ = gidMatch ? ('?gid=' + gidMatch[1]) : '';
      return base + '/preview' + gidQ;
    }
    // Google Docs / Slides : /edit → /preview
    var mDocs = url.match(/^(https:\/\/docs\.google\.com\/(document|presentation|forms)\/d\/[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)\/(edit|view|preview)?.*$/i);
    if (mDocs) return mDocs[1] + '/preview';
    // Google Drive fichier : /view → /preview
    var mDrive = url.match(/^(https:\/\/drive\.google\.com\/file\/d\/[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)\/(view|preview|edit)?.*$/i);
    if (mDrive) return mDrive[1] + '/preview';
    // Google Drive open?id=... → preview via /file/d/.../preview
    var mOpen = url.match(/^https:\/\/drive\.google\.com\/open\?id=([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/i);
    if (mOpen) return 'https://drive.google.com/file/d/' + mOpen[1] + '/preview';
    // Google Drive folder : /folders/ID → /embeddedfolderview?id=ID
    var mFolder = url.match(/^https:\/\/drive\.google\.com\/drive\/(?:u\/\d+\/)?folders\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/i);
    if (mFolder) return 'https://drive.google.com/embeddedfolderview?id=' + mFolder[1] + '#list';
  } catch(e) { /* fallback */ }
  // Pas reconnu → renvoyer tel quel (le navigateur peut bloquer si X-Frame-Options)
  return url;
}
function openCleaningEmbed(rawUrl, title, kind, icon){
  var modal   = document.getElementById('clnEmbedModal');
  var iframe  = document.getElementById('clnEmbedFrame');
  var loader  = document.getElementById('clnEmbedLoading');
  var newTab  = document.getElementById('clnEmbedNewTab');
  var titleEl = document.getElementById('clnEmbedTitle');
  var kindEl  = document.getElementById('clnEmbedKind');
  var badgeEl = document.getElementById('clnEmbedBadge');
  if (!modal || !iframe) return;

  var embedUrl = clnToEmbedUrl(rawUrl);
  titleEl.textContent = title || '—';
  kindEl.textContent  = kind  || 'DOCUMENT';
  if (badgeEl && icon) badgeEl.textContent = icon;
  newTab.href = rawUrl;

  // Loader visible pendant le chargement
  loader.classList.remove('hide');

  // Charger l'iframe
  iframe.onload = function(){ loader.classList.add('hide'); };
  iframe.src = embedUrl;

  openModal('clnEmbedModal');
}
// Quand on ferme un modal contenant une iframe, on vide l'iframe pour stopper la lecture
(function(){
  var prevClose = window.closeModal;
  window.closeModal = function(id){
    if (id === 'clnEmbedModal') {
      var f = document.getElementById('clnEmbedFrame');
      var l = document.getElementById('clnEmbedLoading');
      if (f) f.src = 'about:blank';
      if (l) l.classList.remove('hide');
    }
    if (id === 'incModal') {
      var ef = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteFrame');
      var el = document.getElementById('mIncEnqueteLoading');
      if (ef) ef.src = 'about:blank';
      if (el) el.classList.remove('hide');
    }
    return prevClose ? prevClose(id) : null;
  };
})();

// ── EMBED PROCÉDURES — réutilise le modal iframe générique ──
// Ouvre une procédure HSE (Drive / Docs / Sheets) DANS le dashboard,
// au lieu de basculer sur un nouvel onglet Google Drive.
function openProcedureEmbed(url, title){
  if (!url) return;
  openCleaningEmbed(url, title || 'Procédure HSE', 'PROCÉDURE HSE', '📄');
}

function clearClnFilters(){
  document.getElementById('clnSearch').value = '';
  document.getElementById('clnSort').value   = 'date_desc';
  document.getElementById('clnFilterZone').value = 'all';
  clnStatFilter = 'all';
  document.querySelectorAll('#clnStatChips .tag-filter-chip').forEach(function(c,i){c.classList.toggle('on',i===0);});
  applyClnF();
}
function populateClnDropdowns(){
  if (!D || !D.cleaning) return;
  var empls = {};
  D.cleaning.forEach(function(c){
    var e = (c.emplacement || c.zone || '').trim();
    if (e) empls[e] = (empls[e]||0) + 1;
  });
  var zSel = document.getElementById('clnFilterZone');
  if (zSel) {
    var prev = zSel.value;
    zSel.innerHTML = '<option value="all">Tous</option>' +
      Object.keys(empls).sort().map(function(z){return '<option value="'+esc(z)+'">'+esc(z)+' ('+empls[z]+')</option>';}).join('');
    if (prev) zSel.value = prev;
  }
}
function applyClnF(){
  if (!D || !D.cleaning) return;
  var search    = (document.getElementById('clnSearch').value || '').trim().toLowerCase();
  var sort      = document.getElementById('clnSort').value;
  var fZone     = document.getElementById('clnFilterZone').value;

  var filtered = D.cleaning.filter(function(c){
    if (clnStatFilter === 'open'   && !isClnOpen(c)) return false;
    if (clnStatFilter === 'closed' && !isClnClosed(c)) return false;
    var empl = (c.emplacement || c.zone || '').trim();
    if (fZone !== 'all' && empl !== fZone) return false;
    if (search) {
      var hay = [c.id, empl].join(' ').toLowerCase();
      if (hay.indexOf(search) < 0) return false;
    }
    return true;
  });

  filtered.sort(function(a,b){
    if (sort === 'date_desc') return (b.isoDate||'').localeCompare(a.isoDate||'') || 0;
    if (sort === 'date_asc')  return (a.isoDate||'').localeCompare(b.isoDate||'') || 0;
    if (sort === 'id_asc' || sort === 'id_desc') {
      var na = parseInt(String(a.id).match(/\d+/),10), nb = parseInt(String(b.id).match(/\d+/),10);
      var diff = (isNaN(na)||isNaN(nb)) ? String(a.id).localeCompare(String(b.id)) : (na - nb);
      return sort === 'id_asc' ? diff : -diff;
    }
    if (sort === 'empl_az' || sort === 'zone_az') {
      return (a.emplacement||a.zone||'').localeCompare(b.emplacement||b.zone||'');
    }
    return 0;
  });

  // Stats pills (état dérivé des photos)
  var total  = D.cleaning.length;
  var open   = D.cleaning.filter(isClnOpen).length;
  var closed = D.cleaning.filter(isClnClosed).length;
  var statsRow = document.getElementById('clnStatsRow');
  if (statsRow) {
    statsRow.innerHTML =
      '<span class="tag-stat-pill tsp-total">'+total+' total</span>' +
      '<span class="tag-stat-pill tsp-open">'+open+' en cours</span>' +
      '<span class="tag-stat-pill tsp-closed">'+closed+' terminés</span>' +
      (filtered.length !== total ? '<span class="tag-stat-pill tsp-filtered">'+filtered.length+' filtrés</span>' : '');
  }
  document.getElementById('clnListCount').textContent = filtered.length + ' / ' + total;

  renderClnTable(filtered, search);
}
function renderClnTable(items, searchVal){
  var tb = document.getElementById('clnBody');
  if (!tb) return;
  if (items.length === 0) {
    tb.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="6" style="text-align:center;color:var(--text3);padding:20px">Aucune entrée pour ce filtre</td></tr>';
    return;
  }
  function hl(str){
    if (!searchVal || !str) return esc(str||'');
    var re = new RegExp('('+searchVal.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g,'\\$&')+')','gi');
    return esc(str).replace(re,'<mark style="background:rgba(245,166,35,.35);border-radius:2px;padding:0 1px">$1</mark>');
  }
  tb.innerHTML = '';
  var pendingThumbs = [];   // { fid, imgId } → chargement asynchrone groupé
  items.forEach(function(c, idx){
    var hasAvant = clnHasAvant(c);
    var hasApres = clnHasApres(c);
    var closed   = hasAvant && hasApres;
    var open     = hasAvant && !hasApres;
    var statClass = closed ? 's-close' : (open ? 's-open' : '');
    var statTxt   = closed ? 'Terminé' : (open ? 'En cours' : '—');

    var emplTxt = c.emplacement || c.zone || '—';

    // ── Cellules vignettes Avant / Après ──────────────────────
    function thumbCell(label, has, fid, ref){
      var cellId = 'clnThumb_' + idx + '_' + label;
      if (!has || !fid) {
        return '<td class="cln-thumb-cell"><div class="cln-thumb-ph" title="Pas de photo '+label+'">📷</div></td>';
      }
      pendingThumbs.push({ fid: fid, cellId: cellId, label: label, ref: ref || '', cln: c });
      return '<td class="cln-thumb-cell"><div id="'+cellId+'" class="cln-thumb-load" title="Chargement photo '+label+' depuis Drive…"></div></td>';
    }
    var avantCellHtml = thumbCell('Avant', c.hasPhotoAvant, c.driveFileIdAvant, c.photoRefAvant);
    var apresCellHtml = thumbCell('Après', c.hasPhotoApres, c.driveFileIdApres, c.photoRefApres);

    var tr = document.createElement('tr');
    tr.style.cursor = 'pointer';
    tr.innerHTML =
      '<td style="white-space:nowrap;font-size:10px">'+esc(c.date||'—')+'</td>' +
      avantCellHtml + apresCellHtml +
      '<td><span class="rbadge">'+hl(emplTxt)+'</span></td>' +
      '<td>'+(c.zone ? '<span class="rbadge">'+hl(c.zone)+'</span>' : '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:9px">—</span>')+'</td>' +
      '<td>' + (statTxt === '—' ? '<span style="color:var(--text3);font-size:9px">—</span>' : '<span class="'+statClass+'">'+esc(statTxt)+'</span>') + '</td>';

    tr.addEventListener('click', function(){ openCleanModal(c); });
    tb.appendChild(tr);
  });

  // ── Chargement asynchrone des vignettes (avec cache) ───────────
  if (!window._clnPhotoCache) window._clnPhotoCache = {};
  pendingThumbs.forEach(function(p){
    var slot = document.getElementById(p.cellId);
    if (!slot) return;
    var cached = window._clnPhotoCache[p.fid];
    if (cached) {
      replaceThumb(slot, cached, p);
      return;
    }
    google.script.run
      .withSuccessHandler(function(d){
        if (d) {
          window._clnPhotoCache[p.fid] = d;
          replaceThumb(slot, d, p);
        } else {
          slot.outerHTML = '<div class="cln-thumb-ph" title="Lecture impossible">⚠️</div>';
        }
      })
      .withFailureHandler(function(){
        slot.outerHTML = '<div class="cln-thumb-ph" title="Lecture impossible">⚠️</div>';
      })
      .getTagPhotoForClient(p.fid);
  });
}
function replaceThumb(slot, dataUrl, p){
  if (!slot || !slot.parentNode) return;
  var img = document.createElement('img');
  img.src = dataUrl;
  img.className = 'cln-thumb';
  img.alt = p.label;
  img.title = p.label + (p.ref ? ' · ' + p.ref : '') + ' (cliquer pour agrandir)';
  img.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    e.stopPropagation();
    openCleanModal(p.cln);
    var photoTab = document.querySelectorAll('#cleanModal .modal-tab')[1];
    if (photoTab) switchTab('mCln','photo',photoTab);
  });
  slot.parentNode.replaceChild(img, slot);
}
function openCleanModal(c){
  document.getElementById('mClnId').textContent   = 'NET ' + c.id + (c.date ? ' · ' + c.date : '');
  document.getElementById('mClnDesc').textContent = c.emplacement || c.zone || '—';

  var hasAvant = clnHasAvant(c);
  var hasApres = clnHasApres(c);
  var closed   = hasAvant && hasApres;
  var open     = hasAvant && !hasApres;
  var statTxt  = closed ? 'Terminé' : (open ? 'En cours' : '—');
  var statColor= closed ? 'var(--green)' : (open ? 'var(--red)' : 'var(--text2)');

  var chips  = '';
  if (c.emplacement || c.zone) chips += '<span class="modal-chip">📍 '+esc(c.emplacement||c.zone)+'</span>';
  chips += '<span class="modal-chip" style="color:'+statColor+'">'+esc(statTxt)+'</span>';
  if (hasAvant || hasApres) chips += '<span class="modal-chip" style="color:var(--green)">📸 Drive</span>';
  document.getElementById('mClnChips').innerHTML = chips;

  document.getElementById('mClnInfoGrid').innerHTML = [
    infoItemF('ID',          c.id),
    infoItemF('Date',        c.date || '—'),
    infoItemF('Emplacement', c.emplacement || c.zone || '—'),
    infoItemF('Statut',      statTxt)
  ].join('');

  // ── Photos (Avant + Après) via proxy base64 ─────────────
  var photoArea     = document.getElementById('mClnPhotoArea');
  var photoTabBtn   = document.getElementById('clnPhotoTabBtn');
  var hasAny   = hasAvant || hasApres;

  if (hasAny) {
    if (photoTabBtn) photoTabBtn.textContent = '📸 Photos Drive';
    photoArea.innerHTML =
      '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:14px;padding:48px 20px">' +
      '<div class="spin"></div>' +
      '<p style="color:var(--text3);font-size:12px">Chargement depuis Google Drive…</p>' +
      '</div>';

    var results = { avant: null, apres: null };
    var expected = (hasAvant ? 1 : 0) + (hasApres ? 1 : 0);
    var loaded = 0;

    function renderPhotos(){
      var html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:16px;justify-content:center;width:100%">';
      if (hasAvant) {
        html += '<div style="flex:1;min-width:220px;max-width:48%;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:6px">';
        html += '<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--amber);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.5px;padding:3px 10px;background:rgba(245,166,35,.12);border:1px solid rgba(245,166,35,.3);border-radius:6px">⚠️ Avant</div>';
        if (results.avant) html += '<img src="'+results.avant+'" style="max-width:100%;max-height:44vh;border-radius:10px;object-fit:contain;border:1px solid var(--border)">';
        else html += '<div class="photo-noimg" style="padding:16px"><div style="font-size:28px;margin-bottom:6px">⚠️</div><p style="color:var(--amber);font-size:11px">Lecture impossible</p></div>';
        html += '<p style="font-size:9px;color:var(--text3)">📁 '+esc(c.photoRefAvant||'avant')+'</p></div>';
      }
